function TryWaitForBuffer
{
param(
[Parameter(Position=0)]
[System.Object[]]$tcp,

[Parameter(Position=1)]
[int]$count,
[Parameter(Position=2)]
[int]$timeout
)

$start = [DateTime]::Now;
do
{
if ($tcp.Available -ge $count)
{
return $True;
}
Start-Sleep -Milliseconds 1;
}
while (([DateTime]::Now - $start).TotalSeconds -lt $timeout);
return $False;

}
$sb = {

param( $b64guid, $serverAddress, $serverPort )
function TryWaitForBuffer
{
param(
[Parameter(Position=0)]
[System.Object[]]$tcp,

[Parameter(Position=1)]
[int]$count,
[Parameter(Position=2)]
[int]$timeout
)

$start = [DateTime]::Now;
do
{
if ($tcp.Available -ge $count)
{
return $True;
}
Start-Sleep -Milliseconds 1;
}
while (([DateTime]::Now - $start).TotalSeconds -lt $timeout);
return $False;

}



function HandleClient($sock, $mainTcp) {

$buf = new-object System.Byte[] 8192
$ret = 0;

TryWaitForBuffer($mainTcp, 4, 10);
$recvd = $sock.Receive($buf, 4, 0);

$targetTcp = 0;
Write-Output "Job recvd: $($recvd) av: $($mainTcp.Available) connected: $($mainTcp.Connected)";
if ($recvd -gt 0)
{
if ($buf[0] -eq 5) {

}

$methodCount = $buf[1];

Write-Host "Method count: $($methodCount)";

for ($i = 0; $i -lt $methodCount; $i++)
{
if ($buf[2 + $i] -eq 0) {
$buf[0] = 5;
$buf[1] = 0;
$mainTcp.Client.Send($buf, 2, 0);
break;
}
}
$recvd = $sock.Receive($buf, 4, 0);
if ($recvd -eq 4) {

if ($buf[3] -eq 1) {

$sock.Receive($buf, 4, 0);
[byte[]]$bIpaddress = $buf[0..3];
$intAddress = [BitConverter]::ToUInt32($bIpaddress, 0);
$destAddress = New-Object System.Net.IPAddress($intAddress);
$sock.Receive($buf, 2, 0);
$bPort = $buf[0..1];
[System.Array]::Reverse($bPort);

$port = [BitConverter]::ToUInt16($bPort, 0);
$connectionStatus = ConnectDestinationIpv4 $port $destAddress ([ref]$targetTcp)

Write-Host "Connection $($connectionStatus) to $($destAddress):$($port)"
if ($connectionStatus -eq $False)
{
return -1;
}

$sentStatus = SendResponse $sock $destAddress 4 $port 1
Write-Host "Sent $($sentStatus) to $($destAddress):$($port)"
if ($sentStatus -eq $False) {

return -1;
}
}
elseif ($buf[3] -eq 3) {
TryWaitForBuffer($mainTcp, 1, 10);
$sock.Receive($buf, 1, 0);
$domainNameLen = $buf[0];
TryWaitForBuffer($mainTcp, $domainNameLen, 10);
$sock.Receive($buf, $domainNameLen, 0);

$domainName = [System.Text.Encoding]::UTF8.GetString($buf[0..$domainNameLen]);

Write-Host "Connecting to domain: $($domainName)";

TryWaitForBuffer($mainTcp, 2, 10);

$sock.Receive($buf, 2, 0);
$bPort = $buf[0..1];
[System.Array]::Reverse($bPort);
$port = [BitConverter]::ToUInt16($bPort, 0);
Write-Host "Connecting to port: $($port)"


$destAddress = 0;

ResolveDomain $domainName ([ref]$destAddress);

$connectionStatus = ConnectDestinationIpv4 $port $destAddress ([ref]$targetTcp)

Write-Host "Connection status: $($connectionStatus)";
if ($connectionStatus -eq $False)
{
return -1;
}


$sentStatus = SendResponse $sock $destAddress 4 $port 1
if ($sentStatus -eq $False) {

return -1;
}
}
}
else {
return -1;
}


Write-Host "Goto while";

$targetBuffer = new-object System.Byte[] 4096
$adminBuffer = new-object System.Byte[] 4096
while ($True)
{
if ($mainTcp.Client.Available -gt 0)
{
$count = $mainTcp.Client.Receive($adminBuffer);
$sent = $targetTcp.Client.Send($adminBuffer, 0, $count, 0);
}
if ($targetTcp.Client.Available -gt 0)
{
$count = $targetTcp.Client.Receive($targetBuffer);
$sent = $mainTcp.Client.Send($targetBuffer, 0, $count, 0);
}
Start-Sleep -Milliseconds 1

}

}
}


function ConnectDestinationIpv4($port, $ipaddress, [ref]$targetTcp) {

$targetTcp.value = New-Object System.Net.Sockets.TcpClient($ipaddress, $port);

return $targetTcp.value.Connected;
}

function SendResponse($sock, $destinationAddress, $destinationLen, $destinationPort, $addressType) {
$answer = new-object System.Byte[] 256
$responseHeaderSize =4;

$answer[0] = 5;
$answer[1] = 0;
$answer[2] = 0;
$answer[3] = $addressType;

$addressBytes = $destinationAddress.GetAddressBytes();

[System.Array]::Copy($addressBytes, 0, $answer, 4, $destinationLen );
$offset += 4+$destinationLen;

$portBytes = [BitConverter]::GetBytes($destinationPort);
[System.Array]::Copy($portBytes, 0, $answer, $offset, 2);

$sent = $sock.Send($answer, $offset + 2, 0);
if($sent -lt 1){
return $False;
}
return $True;
}

function ResolveDomain($domainName, [ref]$destAddress) {
Write-Host "Resolved addresses: $([System.Net.Dns]::GetHostAddresses($domainName)[0])"
$destAddress.value = [System.Net.Dns]::GetHostAddresses($domainName)[0];

return $True;
}
Write-Host "Connecting to $($serverAddress)";

$newSock = New-Object System.Net.Sockets.TcpClient($serverAddress, $serverPort);
$guidBytes = [System.Convert]::FromBase64String($b64guid);
$newSock.Client.Send($guidBytes, 16, 0);

HandleClient $newSock.Client $newSock

};




function Connect-SocksServer {
[Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis.SuppressMessageAttribute('PSShouldProcess', '')]
[CmdletBinding()]
Param(
[ValidateNotNullOrEmpty()]
[String]
$Server,

[ValidateNotNullOrEmpty()]
[Int]
$Port
)
PROCESS {

$timeout = 10;
$tcp = New-Object System.Net.Sockets.TcpClient($Server, $Port)
$buffer = new-object System.Byte[] 4096
$guid = [Guid]::Empty;

Write-Output "Connected: $($tcp.Connected)"
$size = 0;
$bSize = [BitConverter]::GetBytes($size);
$sent = $tcp.Client.Send($guid.ToByteArray(), 16, 0);
$sent = $tcp.Client.Send($bSize, 4, 0);

while ($True) {
$newClientComing = TryWaitForBuffer $tcp 16 10

if($newClientComing -eq $False)
{
continue;
}

$rec = $tcp.Client.Receive($buffer, 16, 0);
$b64guid = [System.Convert]::ToBase64String($buffer[0..15])


$job = Start-Job -scriptblock $sb -ArgumentList @($b64guid,$Server,$Port)

}
}
}
